        <div class="share-data" data-description="Searching for Halloween decorating ideas that are more stylish than spooky? Then take a peek at these eleven pretty no-carve pumpkin projects." data-socialimage="http://f.tqn.com/y/smallspaces/1/S/Y/4/-/-/Doily_Pumpkin.jpg" data-socialtitle="11 Stylish No-Carve Pumpkin Projects" data-url="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm" id="content">
         <!--[if gt IE 8]&gt; &lt;!-- -->
         <noscript class="sbs-1" data-hint="Pretty Pumpkin Projects">
          <!-- &lt;![endif]-->
          <div class="sbs-active-container active-step-1">
           <div class="sbs-intro" id="contentIntro">
            <div class="row">
             <div class="col col-6">
              <span class="page-count">
               1
               <span class="page-count-divider">
                of
               </span>
               11
              </span>
              <a class="show-all" data-component="stepbystepPagination" data-ordinal="ShowAll" data-source="StepContent_Pagination" data-type="" href="#showall">
               Show All
              </a>
              <h2 class="heading ">
               Pretty Pumpkin Projects
              </h2>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figure class="content-img">
             <div class="sbs-img-frame">
              <div class="sbs-prev-next-top">
               <div class="page-btns group small">
                <div class="col pull-left prev">
                 <span class="btn btn-light disabled">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-gray-left">
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="col pull-right next">
                 <a class="ajax-link-sbs" data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Next" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm#step2">
                 </a>
                 <span class="btn p-b-col">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-right">
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="sbs-img-wrapper expandable collapsed">
               <div class="content-img-wrapper no-caption">
                <div class="image-pinit-wrapper">
                 <img alt="Doily_Pumpkin.jpg - Mitzismiscellany.com" class=" addPinit" data-description="11 Stylish No-Carve Pumpkin Projects: Pretty Pumpkin Projects" itemprop="image" src="http://f.tqn.com/y/smallspaces/1/S/Y/4/-/-/Doily_Pumpkin.jpg"/>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </figure>
            <figcaption class="content-img-subtitle">
             <div class="content-img-caption">
              <span class="credit">
               Photo Credit: Mitzismiscellany.com
              </span>
             </div>
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Searching for Halloween decorating ideas that are more stylish than spooky? Thentake a peek atthese eleven prettyno-carve pumpkin projects. EachDIYcan give your fall decor a boo-tiful boost without theghoulishmessgutting pumpkins creates.
             </p>
             <p>
              First up, a
              <strong>
              </strong>
              crochet covered pumpkin.
              <strong>
              </strong>
              This charming project was whipped up Mitzi Curi,the crafty blogger behind Mitzi's Collectibles. She gave a dried gourd a sweet vintage twist usingcrochetdoilies.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://www.mitzismiscellany.com/page/46/">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>
           </article>
           <div class="s-btns s-btns-eoc js-share">
            <a class="s-btn bg-facebook" data-component="shareButtonsEndofContent" data-network="facebook" data-ordinal="1" data-pin-do="skipLink" data-source="Social_ShareEndofContent" data-type="shareFacebook" href="#" title="Share on Facebook">
             <div class="long wrapper">
              <div class="item v-middle">

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Looking for a clever conversation piece for your Halloween
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" href="/od/Blog/tp/5-Easy-to-Make-Hard-Cider-Cocktails-That-Use-3-or-Fewer-Ingredients.htm">
               cocktail
              </a>
              party?KariAnne, at Thistlewood Farms,usedchalkboard paint tocreatea pumpkin centerpiece that doubles as a festive word game.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="2" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://www.thistlewoodfarms.com/chalkboard-word-find-pumpkin">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              If you're not a
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" href="/od/Pets-in-Small-Spaces/ss/How-to-Knit-a-Lions-Mane-for-Your-Dog.htm">
               Halloween
              </a>
              person, check out this pretty idea.Rachel, the blogger who pens the site Lines Across, created a string art pumpkin that shows she hearts fall.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="2" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://www.linesacross.com/2013/10/pumpkin-string-art.html">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Here's a bewitching idea. Alex and Paige,the dynamic duo behind Whimsy Darling,gussied up their pumpkin withblack paint and orange crystals.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://whimsydarling.com/pumpkin-decorating/">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>

              <h2 class="heading ">
               Punky Pumpkins
              </h2>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figure class="content-img">
             <div class="sbs-img-frame">
              <div class="sbs-prev-next-top">
               <div class="page-btns group small">
                <div class="col pull-left prev">
                 <a class="btn p-b-col ajax-link-sbs" data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Prev" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm#step4">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-left">
                  </span>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div class="col pull-right next">
                 <a class="ajax-link-sbs" data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Next" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm#step6">
                 </a>
                 <span class="btn p-b-col">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-right">
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="sbs-img-wrapper expandable collapsed">
               <div class="content-img-wrapper no-caption">
                <div class="image-pinit-wrapper">
                 <img alt="gold_studded_pumpkins_Cuckoo4Design.jpg - Cuckoo4design.com" class=" addPinit" data-description="11 Stylish No-Carve Pumpkin Projects: Punky Pumpkins" itemprop="image" src="http://f.tqn.com/y/smallspaces/1/S/b/4/-/-/gold_studded_pumpkins_Cuckoo4Design.jpg"/>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </figure>
            <figcaption class="content-img-subtitle">
             <div class="content-img-caption">
              <span class="credit">
               Photo Credit: Cuckoo4design.com
              </span>
             </div>
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Want to channel your inner Joan Jett? Julia, the DIY mommy who writes the blogFollow ThisCuckoo, gave abunch of Heirloom pumpkins the punk rock treatment. After giving each gourd a few licks of paints, she rocked them out with brassstuds.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://www.cuckoo4design.com/2013/10/studded-chalk-paint-pumpkins.html">
              </a>
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="2" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://whimsydarling.com/pumpkin-decorating/">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>
           </article>

              <h2 class="heading ">
               A Yarn Wrapped Pumpkin
              </h2>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figure class="content-img">
             <div class="sbs-img-frame">
              <div class="sbs-prev-next-top">
               <div class="page-btns group small">
                <div class="col pull-left prev">
                 <a class="btn p-b-col ajax-link-sbs" data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Prev" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm#step5">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-left">
                  </span>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div class="col pull-right next">
                 <a class="ajax-link-sbs" data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Next" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm#step7">

                 <span class="btn p-b-col">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-right">

                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="sbs-img-wrapper expandable collapsed">
               <div class="content-img-wrapper no-caption">
                <div class="image-pinit-wrapper">
                 <img alt="Yarn_Bomb.jpg - Freepeople.com" class=" addPinit" data-description="11 Stylish No-Carve Pumpkin Projects: A Yarn Wrapped Pumpkin" itemprop="image" src="http://f.tqn.com/y/smallspaces/1/S/e/4/-/-/Yarn_Bomb.jpg"/>
                </div>

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Yarn bombing can give your pumpkin a festive homespun look. You can find the details and instructions for two more no-carve pumpkin projectson the Free People blog.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://blog.freepeople.com/2013/10/alternative-pumpkin-decorations/">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>

              <h2 class="heading ">
               A Sequined Pumpkin
              </h2>
             </div>
            </div>

             <div class="sbs-img-frame">

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Who knew that glaming up a pumpkin could be this easy?Alison Strangposted her dazzling goth sequined project on Whimsey Box.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="https://whimseybox.com/projects/diy-sequined-pumpkin">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              Here's an idea that can dress up your
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" href="/od/Decor/ss/7-Smart-Space-Saving-Tables.htm">
               dining table
              </a>
              forHalloween and Thanksgiving. Melanie, from the site,Find It Make It Love It, crafted this fabulous foliagepumpkin using a glue gun.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="2" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://www.instructables.com/id/DIY-No-carve-typography-pumpkins/">
               tutorial.
              </a>
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="3" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://finditmakeitloveit.com/2013/10/no-carve-pumpkin-ideas.html">
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>

           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              You won't believe what was used to glitz up these pumpkins...wait for it... brass tacks! Shannon, from Madigan Made,whipped up this thumb-tackular
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" href="/od/DIY/ss/Decorating-Small-Spaces-3-Practical-and-Stylish-Projects.htm">
               DIY
              </a>
              project.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="2" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://http//www.madiganmade.com/2011/09/gold-thumbtack-covered-pumpkins-for.html%20the%20glided%20treatment">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>

              <h2 class="heading ">
               Decoupage Pumpkins
              </h2>
             </div>
            </div>
            <figure class="content-img">
             <div class="sbs-img-frame">
              <div class="sbs-prev-next-top">
               <div class="page-btns group small">
                <div class="col pull-left prev">
                 <a class="btn p-b-col ajax-link-sbs" data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Prev" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/DIY/ss/11-Stylish-No-Carve-Pumpkins-Ideas.htm#step10">
                  <span class="sprite arrow5-left">
                  </span>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div class="col pull-right next">
                 <a data-component="stepbystepImage" data-ordinal="Next" data-source="stepbystepImage" data-type="" href="http://smallspaces.about.com/od/Pets-in-Small-Spaces/ss/How-to-Knit-a-Lions-Mane-for-Your-Dog.htm">
                 </a>

                  <span class="sprite arrow5-right">
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="sbs-img-wrapper expandable collapsed">
               <div class="content-img-wrapper no-caption">
                <div class="image-pinit-wrapper">
                 <img alt="decoupage-pumpkins-diy.jpg - Todayscreativeblog.net" class=" addPinit" data-description="11 Stylish No-Carve Pumpkin Projects: Decoupage Pumpkins" itemprop="image" src="http://f.tqn.com/y/smallspaces/1/S/g/4/-/-/decoupage-pumpkins-diy.jpg"/>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </figure>
            <figcaption class="content-img-subtitle">
             <div class="content-img-caption">
              <span class="credit">
               Photo Credit: Todayscreativeblog.net
              </span>
             </div>
            </figcaption>
           </div>
           <article class="sbs content widget expert-content">
            <div class="expert-content-text">
             <p>
              The best part about decoupage is that you can work with anything that's paper thin from printed images to real leaves. Kim Demmon from Today's Creative Blog didbothusing Mod Podge. FYI, she says if you plan to stick your finished pumpkin outside, decoupage with Mod Podge's outdoor formula.
             </p>
             <p>
              <strong>
               Want to DIY?
              </strong>
              Here's the
              <a data-component="link" data-ordinal="1" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="externalLink" href="http://todayscreativeblog.net/no-carve-decoupaged-pumpkins/">
               tutorial.
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>
